     <main class="content" itemprop="mainContentOfPage" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Blog" role="main">
      <article class="post-173 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-free-downloads category-giant-lego-minifigurine category-lego-bean-bags category-lego-birthday-party category-lego-brick-cake category-lego-city-party category-lego-party-decorations category-lego-party-favors category-lego-party-kid-activities category-minifigure-marshmallow-pops entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         LEGO Birthday Party!
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2014-09-10T07:00:00+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
          September 10, 2014
         </time>
         By
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://www.thescrapshoppeblog.com/author/mmscrapshoppe" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Michele McDonald
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="http://www.thescrapshoppeblog.com/2014/09/lego-birthday-party.html#comments">
           4 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-3LssitQsPLA/VA9pJ3UJPQI/AAAAAAAAdZg/3t-pH4Upr6I/s1600/lego-party-table.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="502" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-3LssitQsPLA/VA9pJ3UJPQI/AAAAAAAAdZg/3t-pH4Upr6I/s1600/lego-party-table.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         We survived!! Over the weekend we threw our first family AND friends birthday party. Luckily the weather cooperated (
         <i>
          for the most part
         </i>
         ) so we werent all squished indoors together. We take parties seriously around here so were talking immediate family, grandparents, aunts, uncles, cousins, great aunts, great-grandparents, best friends of mine and the hubs with their kids in attendance and thats just the usual company!! This year we added an additional 6 friends with their parents and siblings. Quite the crowd!!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         My big 6 year old wanted a Lego-themed birthday party this year. He is crazy for those little bricks! He specified a Lego City party so, where I could, I focused more on the City characters. Everything else was straight up Lego bricks!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <p>
         <a name="more">
         </a>
        </p>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-P9EcsitGUl0/VA9pmzpMLFI/AAAAAAAAdZ8/lYRVz3yphEM/s1600/lego-party-invite.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-P9EcsitGUl0/VA9pmzpMLFI/AAAAAAAAdZ8/lYRVz3yphEM/s1600/lego-party-invite.jpg" width="484"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I shared the
         <a href="http://www.thescrapshoppeblog.com/2014/09/lego-birthday-invitations.html" target="_blank">
          Lego birthday invitation
         </a>
         last week. It also played a role in some of the decor for the party as youll soon see.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-5KLPaZ6FHKo/VA9pFgH1L9I/AAAAAAAAdYM/VWiLFI1U150/s1600/lego-birthday-party-table.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="434" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-5KLPaZ6FHKo/VA9pFgH1L9I/AAAAAAAAdYM/VWiLFI1U150/s1600/lego-birthday-party-table.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         Our main colors for the party were red, blue, and yellow. Very similar to our
         <a href="http://www.thescrapshoppeblog.com/2012/09/superhero-party.html" target="_blank">
          Superhero Party
         </a>
         a couple of years ago! I used a yellow cardboard presentation board as the backdrop, but trimmed it down by 8-10.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         The Lego banners are made from foam rectangles that you can purchase at craft stores or even Walmart. You get a stack of 50 for ~$6. I cut circles out of some of the sheets and glued them to other intact sheets of the foam.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         The Lego bricks on the table are gift-wrap covered
         <a href="http://amzn.to/1p4e4S7" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          cardboard blocks
         </a>
         . The gift wrap was only $.99 per roll at Party City. I spray painted candy cups to match the red and blue gift wrap and set them upside down on top of the blocks to look like Lego bricks.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--P56z9QjJts/VA9pIo3GEmI/AAAAAAAAdZU/Ja6pNvha-l8/s1600/lego-party-drinks.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="462" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--P56z9QjJts/VA9pIo3GEmI/AAAAAAAAdZU/Ja6pNvha-l8/s1600/lego-party-drinks.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I had a large drink dispenser full of lemonade alongside a large stack of plain yellow paper cups. I put a note on custom made stationary for guests to draw their own Lego faces on the cups and left several Sharpies to be used.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I wrapped water bottles and juice boxes with the craft foam and glued on more foam circles to look like Lego bricks. I love this because the foam can get wet in a bucket of ice and be completely unaffected.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lzNpJAQ7Ez0/VA9zTmVSA_I/AAAAAAAAdaM/-zSHcra5vEE/s1600/lego-minifigure-head-marshmallow-pops.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="608" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lzNpJAQ7Ez0/VA9zTmVSA_I/AAAAAAAAdaM/-zSHcra5vEE/s1600/lego-minifigure-head-marshmallow-pops.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I shared my
         <a href="http://www.thescrapshoppeblog.com/2014/09/the-best-gummy-recipe.html" target="_blank">
          gummy recipe
         </a>
         earlier this week. We also had pre-prepared
         <a href="http://amzn.to/1opBxhg" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          brick candy
         </a>
         , and some super yummy Lego minifigure marshmallow pops. We made the marshmallow pops by placing large marshmallows on lollipop sticks then dipping them in yellow candy melts. Cut a mini marshmallow in half and place one half on top of the dipped marshmallow. Use a toothpick to cover the mini marshmallow in candy melts.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I cut the lid flaps off of colorful take-out boxes then punched 1 circles in them and adhered them back onto the front of the take-out boxes with 3-D foam tape.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         For the forks and napkins we made a fun holder out of, what else, Legos!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <i>
          Psssst! I also embossed the napkins!
         </i>
         That may seem a little extreme but, honestly, 40 napkins took about 10 minutes to emboss. I was able to emboss two at time, and they turned out SUPER cute!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I didnt even cry when people wiped their mouths on them! 
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cBAnC3wldGw/VA9pGTcMZVI/AAAAAAAAdYc/9_S_JmRlX6M/s1600/lego-brick-birthday-cake.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="366" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cBAnC3wldGw/VA9pGTcMZVI/AAAAAAAAdYc/9_S_JmRlX6M/s1600/lego-brick-birthday-cake.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         Ive started putting together my cakes the day before the party. It is SUCH a game changer!! Its feels SO nice to have the cake in the fridge and ready to be pulled out and put straight on the table on party day.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         For this cake I made a red Lego brick out of
         <a href="http://www.creationsbykara.com/2013/08/easy-pound-cake-recipe.html/" target="_blank">
          pound cake
         </a>
         and marshmallows. The red icing is
         <a href="http://www.thepinningmama.com/2013/08/05/the-worlds-best-buttercream-frosting-recipe/" target="_blank">
          buttercream
         </a>
         .
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I set the scene with my sons Lego City vehicles and characters to make it look like they had constructed the cake themselves. I even had little Lego bricks made from pound cake and mini marshmallows!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-6TKpYB5_JzY/VA9pFnkJRtI/AAAAAAAAdYQ/Pwrydy1KQLk/s1600/inside-lego-cake.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-6TKpYB5_JzY/VA9pFnkJRtI/AAAAAAAAdYQ/Pwrydy1KQLk/s1600/inside-lego-cake.jpg" width="494"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         The cake itself was made up of 3 different pound cakes that had been colored yellow, red, and blue respectively. I cut them into small rectangles then laid them out to form the cake. The cake was 3 layers high with yellow buttercream icing between the layers.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         It was a fun surprise as we cut into the cake to reveal the layers!! It looked like the cake was made of Legos!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-C-lOnzXKtfc/VA9pH89svJI/AAAAAAAAdY8/Ik_BIDEAonU/s1600/lego-party-decorations.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="534" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-C-lOnzXKtfc/VA9pH89svJI/AAAAAAAAdY8/Ik_BIDEAonU/s1600/lego-party-decorations.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I used our old easel chalkboard to make a greeting for our little builders. I had also made two large Lego minifigures for the party decor. More on them in a moment.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         The best, an most inexpensive, Lego party decor was on the front door and the party table backdrop.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I picked up a plastic tablecloth with a matching set of plates. For the door, I trimmed the tablecloth to be the same size as the door and taped it on. I then taped the plates to the door to look like a giant Lego. SO easy, pretty inexpensive, and a big impact!!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         For the party table backdrop I did the same as with the door, trimming the tablecloth to fit the window and taping it down. I saw this awesome technique when perusing ideas on Pinterest. You can check out all of the fun things I found on this
         <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/mmscrapshoppe/party-inspiration-gavin/" target="_blank">
          party board
         </a>
         .
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-zEwkHqyP744/VA9pIHjd-BI/AAAAAAAAdY4/iHebZrYwIcE/s1600/lego-minifigure.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="518" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-zEwkHqyP744/VA9pIHjd-BI/AAAAAAAAdY4/iHebZrYwIcE/s1600/lego-minifigure.jpg" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         Back to the giant foam minifigure! I bought oversized sheets of foam in red, blue, and yellow. For the hair a regular 8.511 sheet of brown (
         <i>
          or other hair color
         </i>
         )will work. I made a template (
         <i>
          which I am sharing with you!
         </i>
         ) which you print on 3 sheets of paper. Cut out the template and trace it onto the foam, cut it out, and tape/glue the pieces together.The shirt is too large to fit on a regular piece of printed paper so you can print half then flip it over to trace the other half.Draw the face, lines on the shirt and pants, and youre done!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         Click the links below to download the files. The Lego minifig will be just under 2 feet in length.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="https://app.box.com/s/1ewcxqxizl63hgoqwbrr" target="_blank">
          Head
         </a>
         |
         <a href="https://app.box.com/s/iqomlhgb9j7ciaidd6xj" target="_blank">
          Shirt
         </a>
         |
         <a href="https://app.box.com/s/b9sjbmmq4xzz9nln4nbd" target="_blank">
          Pants
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         He matches perfectly with the minifigure on the birthday invitation!!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-f_86In8IzHU/VA9pKAITGdI/AAAAAAAAdZk/gD__5qD2jVc/s1600/lego-patent-print-posters.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="410" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-f_86In8IzHU/VA9pKAITGdI/AAAAAAAAdZk/gD__5qD2jVc/s1600/lego-patent-print-posters.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I found these awesome
         <a href="http://amzn.to/1wftYim" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          patent prints
         </a>
         on Amazon and had to have them. Well end up hanging them in the play room now that the party is over, but arent they amazing?
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DIWgXeop1JI/VA9pHjrDlOI/AAAAAAAAdY0/oxR-uZstVfw/s1600/lego-party-activities.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="520" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DIWgXeop1JI/VA9pHjrDlOI/AAAAAAAAdY0/oxR-uZstVfw/s1600/lego-party-activities.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         As far as activities for the kids, we went to the Lego store to pick up parts for all of the kids to make their own Lego cars. We had made cars of them ahead of time and took photos of them (
         <i>
          then took them all back apart, of course
         </i>
         ) and printed them out to scatter around the table for inspiration.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         The Lego website has a TON of games and activities. I found some Lego City coloring pages and had them printed at my local copy store for the kids to color. I also made a blank Lego minifigure and had it printed as well for the kids to color. They
         <i>
          really
         </i>
         enjoyed that! They were super creative. You can download the Lego minifigure
         <a href="https://app.box.com/s/m2qragegzy2i1od134kt" target="_blank">
          here
         </a>
         .
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I had also purchased a bunch of plastic construction hats and made stickers for each that said Master Brick Builder.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--k5apflZHUo/VA9pJN2HryI/AAAAAAAAdZQ/ayvOelxeG3U/s1600/lego-party-fun.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="542" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--k5apflZHUo/VA9pJN2HryI/AAAAAAAAdZQ/ayvOelxeG3U/s1600/lego-party-fun.jpg" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         Once again we rented a couple of bounce houses for the party. Its such a great way to keep the kids entertained! Not to mention wear them out. We were even able to rent these off of Craiglist which kept the cost down, and we had them for 48 hours. LOTS of extra play time for my two boys!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         Are you following me on
         <a href="http://instagram.com/mmscrapshoppe" target="_blank">
          Instagram
         </a>
         ? If so, you may have recognized several of the photos Ive shared already. Including this Lego bean bag! I borrowed corn hole boards from my sis-in-law and made these Lego bean bags out of felt to use. Great entertainment for the kids AND adults!
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         Also, I am no good at corn hole. 
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-l-mlr0eISWM/VA9pI42TlYI/AAAAAAAAdZM/jqX-X1HFHV8/s1600/lego-party-favor-bag.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-l-mlr0eISWM/VA9pI42TlYI/AAAAAAAAdZM/jqX-X1HFHV8/s1600/lego-party-favor-bag.JPG" width="464"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I used these red paper bags for the party favors. I cut circles out of red cardstock and used 3-D foam tape to adhere them to the bags.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         The bags were filled with a yo-yo, Lego minifigure (
         <i>
          purchased as a batch on Ebay
         </i>
         ), Skittles, Lego eraser (
         <i>
          set of 4 for $.88 at Target!
         </i>
         ), and a notepad that I changed the cover to look like a Lego (
         <i>
          more of those foam sheets!
         </i>
         ).
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I made custom thank you tags to match the stationary and Lego invitation.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OeIiclG1BBM/VA9pFoxJwrI/AAAAAAAAdYU/c1un36Ku9vs/s1600/lego-birthday-boy.JPG" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="508" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OeIiclG1BBM/VA9pFoxJwrI/AAAAAAAAdYU/c1un36Ku9vs/s1600/lego-birthday-boy.JPG" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         I was so proud of my birthday boy! He was super gracious to all of his guests.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         And I think that smile says it all!! I am one happy mama that he is this happy.
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         And a big thank you to all of the amazing family members who always help me make these parties a success! You know who you are! 
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
